using System;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;

namespace Sample1
{
    class Class1
    {
        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            try
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Hello World!");
            }
            catch(Exception ex)
            {
                try
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("Exception occured");
                }
                catch
                {
                    //nested catch
                    /*nesting catch comment*/
                }
            }
        }
    }
    class Class2
    {
        string Filecontent;
        static int ClassValue;
        public void Main(int param1,bool param2,string param3, Method1 param4)
        {
            int Salary=1000;
            decimal=20M;
            string name="John Williams";
            try
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Hello World!");
            }
            catch(Exception ex)
            {}

            try
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Hello World!");
            }
            catch(Exception ex)
            {
            //empty comment block.
            }
    	}
    }
    interface IDesign
    {
        string textboxValue { get; set; };
        void setDesign(string param);
        string getDesign();
    }
}

        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            try
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Hello World!");
            }
            catch(Exception ex)
            {
                try
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("Exception occured");
                }
                catch
                {
                    //nested catch
                    /*nesting catch comment*/
                }
            }
        }
    }
    class Class2
    {
        string Filecontent;
        static int ClassValue;
        public void Main(int param1,bool param2,string param3, Method1 param4)
        {
            int Salary=1000;
            decimal=20M;
            string name="John Williams";
            try
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Hello World!");
            }
            catch(Exception ex)
            {}

            try
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Hello World!");
            }
            catch(Exception ex)
            {
            //empty comment block.
            }
    	}
    }
    interface IDesign
    {
        string textboxValue { get; set; };
        void setDesign(string param);
        string getDesign();
    }
}

        string textboxValue { get; set; };
        void setDesign(string param);
        string getDesign();
    }
}namespace Sample500
{
    class Class1
    {
        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            try
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Hello World!");
            }
            catch(Exception ex)
            {
                try
                {
                    Console.WriteLine("Exception occured");
                }
                catch
                {
                    //nested catch
                    /*nesting catch comment*/
                }
            }
        }
    }
    class Class2
    {
        string Filecontent;
        static int ClassValue;
        public void Main(int param1,bool param2,string param3, Method1 param4)
        {
            int Salary=1000;
            decimal=20M;
            string name="John Williams";
            try
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Hello World!");
            }
            catch(Exception ex)
            {}

            try
            {
                Console.WriteLine("Hello World!");
            }
            catch(Exception ex)
            {
            //empty comment block.
            }
    	}
    }
    interface IDesign
    {
        string textboxValue { get; set; };
        void setDesign(string param);
        string getDesign();
    }
}
